                                            SUBWAY ENVIRONMENT SIMULATION
                                                  SIMULATION OF
                         SES v4.1 file with a simple rail tunnel (up line, down line, one station).
                         Normal operations case in which the pressure caused by moving trains causes
                         a fan to blow up and stop the run.  This causes simulation error type 6.
                         This run also has a fire (unsteady heat gain, form 4) in a non-fire run
                         and can be used to check the correct processing of those.
                         SESconv.py can process the .TMP file and show the user what's going
                         on up until the timestep before the run crashes.
                                    DESIGN TIME 1700 HRS   JULY       2029
